The backlash continued with state-owned television CCTV scrapping its plans to broadcast pre-season games in Shanghai and Shenzhen, and the cancellation of other promotional fan events. The league issued an apology, though NBA Commissioner Adam Silver angered Chinese officials further when he defended the right of players and team executives to free speech. China represents a lucrative market for the NBA, which stands to lose millions of dollars in revenue and threatens to alienate Chinese fans. 该咨询向该市提出了13项建议，包括建立一个针对短期租赁房东的收费注册系统，如果房东未进行注册，将对其处以每天最高$ 1,000的罚.........<br><img align="bottom" src="http://www.epochtimes.com/assets/themes/djy/images/time.gif"> 2019年10月13日 7:25 AM			</td></tr>
